Open BethINI from the \u003ccode\u003eTools\u003c/code\u003e folder inside your LitR installation folder.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eSetup\u003c/code\u003e tab\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCheck that the game path is pointing to the folder called \u003ccode\u003eStock Game Folder\u003c/code\u003e, inside your installation folder and not your steam installation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCheck that the mod organizer path is pointing to the modorganizer.exe in your installation folder for Life in the Ruins.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCheck that your game settings path is set to \u003ccode\u003emy documents/my games/fallout 4\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eBasic\u003c/code\u003e Tab\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eChoose a profile at least one step lower than you would use for vanilla fallout. For most users with less than a 3090 I recommend medium or high, LitR is significantly heavier than vanilla fallout. (The shorter draw distances on medium make A Forest much easier to run, and A Forest makes it so you can't see stuff way in the distance anyway)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor most users, 1920x1080 resolution is recommended.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnable \u003ccode\u003eVSync\u003c/code\u003e unless you're using Gsync/FreeSync (the \u003ccode\u003eHigh FPS Physics Fix\u003c/code\u003e mod controls VSync and this settings should be ignored, but having it match here doesn't hurt)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOn the custom tab, select \u003ccode\u003egeneral\u003c/code\u003e in the section drop down, and \u003ccode\u003eiNumHWThreads\u003c/code\u003e in the settings drop down. Set this to the number of cores your CPU has, doubling that number if it has hyperthreading. For more information on this setting, see \u003ca href=\"https://stepmodifications.org/wiki/Guide:Skyrim_INI/General#iNumHWThreads\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ehttps://stepmodifications.org/wiki/Guide:Skyrim_INI/General#iNumHWThreads\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eDetails\u003c/code\u003e tab\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eField of View (FOV)\nIt is recommended to leave the FoV vanilla. Setting the FoV higher than 90 has been known to cause weird visual issues with armor mods in the list. It can also effect the pipboy and scopes. Do not use the game console to change the FOV, it will not work.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 aware of\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eVSync settings MUST be set to application controlled\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDisable any framerate caps or dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn the ENB section, are three presets to enable ENBoost 8k, 12k, and 16k, with the required files edited and ready to use, all you have to do is enable one of them. See these videos for help choosing what value works best for you.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y4cz-lFXDo8\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eIntroduction to ENBoost\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xSz84F1kgkM\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eHow to find your optimal value with ENBoost\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eHigher values might work for users with a lot of VRAM, but are unnecessary. For most users this will actually reduce performance and stability. Even with high res textures, FO4 doesn't require that much memory.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eENBoost is a feature of ENB that allows your FO4 to extend your system's VRAM with your regular RAM. It's not as fast, but it's better than nothing. AMD users with resizable BAR enabled should see even better performance improvements with this setting, and it's recommended to try it out. However this is a HIGHLY system specific setting. What works great for a user with a 3090, will crash for a user with less, which is why it's not turned on for you by default.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you have issues with textures not loading, stuttering, or the brown face bug, it is recommended to try this.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDifficulty and Customization\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor People that want to tweak things a little. For players who want a real challenge.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eHome Unimprovement - Vanilla Crafting\u003c/code\u003e : for people who want vanilla settlement\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eAbandoned Hub\u003c/code\u003e - an undeground hub settlement, provided as a fast travel alternative\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConfiguration\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAdditional configuration options\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e120FPS no VSYNC\u003c/code\u003e: Enable this mod if you are using a higher refresh rate Gsync/Freesync monitor.  This mod increases the FPS cap from the High Performance Physics Fix mod  and disables vsync.  You can edit the ini file if you need additional changes, or create you own configuration file.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eWhisky's Tunes\u003c/code\u003e: Copyright free music for 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eLaunch modorganizer.exe from the Life in the Ruins installation If it seems frozen, try alt-tabbing a couple times.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStart a new survival game (strongly recommended, but not required).  The list is balanced around survival.  There are options in the MCM in game to adjust survival settings and damage settings.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eMod Configuration Menu\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMCM Settings Manager: Load the LitR Default settings\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eOnce you're out of the vault, use the Beantown Interiors Settings holotape to enable Hardcore Clutter, and Disable The Mad Bomber's Workshop and Collectibles crafting (these are recommended settings, but aren't required)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eUpdating the Modlist\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-updating-the-modlist\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Updating the Modlist\" href=\"#updating-the-modlist\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBefore updating the modlist, \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/changelog.md\"\u003esee the full changelog\u003c/a\u003e for the latest release. Make sure to follow any additional instructions in the changelog regarding the update process. If an update is marked as save safe, then a new save is not required.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo Update the modlist, just rerun the Wabbajack installer with the updated download from the Wabbajack gallery (or prerelease from my Patreon). Check \"overwrite\" during the installation process.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eYou do not need to rerun Bethini, as with Life in the Ruins the the game settings are stored in your my documents folder, not inside the list. However, it does no harm to check everything is still setup as expected.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eYou do need to reapply any MCM settings that you changed. If you're making extensive MCM changes, it is recommended to export these and back them up outside your LitR install before updating.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you still have the downloads, Wabbajack will detect them and you will not need to download the entire modlist again, and the process should just take a couple minutes. If you deleted them, then yes, you will need to download all the files again.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eKnown Issues\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-known-issues\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Known Issues\" href=\"#known-issues\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePerformance Issues: Infinite Loading Screens, Micro Stuttering, Textures not loading, or the Brown Face bug:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eStop other processes to free up RAM, browser windows are especially a problem here\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTry setting the resolution to 1920x1080 if you're running above that\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure you've set iNumHWThreads, as specified in the Bethini section of this readme.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSS2 script failures on new game are the result of going through the opening sequence too quickly. After you finish character creation, wait for 30 seconds or so before exiting the bathroom.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCrashing\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMedal.TV is incompatible with ENB, disable one or the other.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eInfinite Loading Screen\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHaving your config ini's synced to one-drive. To use it simply run the Crash Log Scanner from the dropdown in MO2.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDisable the \u003ccode\u003eFCX Mode\u003c/code\u003e option in the scanner\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePress the Scan Crash Logs button.  The scanner will automatically copy your crash logs over to it's own folder and scan them.  If your crash logs are not in the default location for some reason, you can use the Custom Scan Folder browse button to set the path.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe script will throw a lot of warnings in the \u003ccode\u003eCHECKING FOR MODS THAT CAN CAUSE FREQUENT CRASHES...\u003c/code\u003e. These can all be safely ignored, I have already dealt with all of them. You do not need to make any modifications to the mod list to deal with CTDs- these are almost always either random instability (which is expected in heavily modded FO4, but should be minimal), mis-configurations on the user end, or modifications that the user has made to the list.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSee the readme.md in the tools\\Classic Portable js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Life In The Ruins: A Selection of Lunar Fallout Plus Modlists</h1><a id="user-content-life-in-the-ruins-a-selection-of-lunar-fallout-plus-modlists" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Life In The Ruins: A Selection of Lunar Fallout Plus Modlists" href="#life-in-the-ruins-a-selection-of-lunar-fallout-plus-modlists"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A massively overhauled and finely tuned Fallout 4 experience. Designed to rebalance the game so that the challenge comes primarily from scarcity of resources, while staying true to the vanilla aesthetic. With options for a more vanilla+ style playthrough, as well as an even more challenging survival experience.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://discord.gg/HUNWVBjZPg" rel="nofollow">Join the Community on Discord</a>
<a href="https://www.patreon.com/user?u=4257489" rel="nofollow">Support me on Patreon</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Modlist Goals</h2><a id="user-content-modlist-goals" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Modlist Goals" href="#modlist-goals"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Difficulty comes from scarcity of resources, not bullet sponges.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">RPG Balance, Scaling, and Progression - brought to you by Lunar Fallout Overhaul.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Strategic rather than tactical combat - prepare in advance for difficult encounters, instead of respawning until you get it right.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A vibrant, forested, inhabited, and uncivilized wasteland. Neglected areas should feel fleshed out, but it should still feel lonely.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">New Uniques - almost every single quest reward and vendor unique is now a modded weapon or armor.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Extra high-quality content with the same style and tone as vanilla (no pointlessly skimpy outfits, no tacti-cool weapons).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Full controller support (no extra configuration required).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Smooth performance on mid-range modern gaming hardware.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">This is not...</h3><a id="user-content-this-is-not" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: This is not..." href="#this-is-not"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A hardcore, nitty-gritty, track-everything-with-a-spreadsheet survival simulator</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A tactical shooter</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Fallout New Vegas</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A good base-list for building on top of - if you want that try Welcome to Paradise or Fusion</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A modlist that has every mod on the nexus- this is a huge list, but everything in it is hand picked, and carefully integrated to provide a focused experience, based around an enhanced and expanded vanilla game.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Optional Creation Club Content Compatibility</h3><a id="user-content-optional-creation-club-content-compatibility" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Optional Creation Club Content Compatibility" href="#optional-creation-club-content-compatibility"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li><a href="https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/CreationClubContent.md">Weapons and Armour Skins</a> Faction Distribution Framework will distribute faction based weapon and armour skins into the world- see the link for more details</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://loadorderlibrary.com/lists/life-in-the-ruins-2" rel="nofollow">Full List of Mods at LoadOrderLibrary</a></h3><a id="user-content-full-list-of-mods-at-loadorderlibrary" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Full List of Mods at LoadOrderLibrary" href="#full-list-of-mods-at-loadorderlibrary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Things you should know...</h2><a id="user-content-things-you-should-know" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Things you should know..." href="#things-you-should-know"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Check out the <a href="https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/LitR%20Tips%20and%20Tricks.md">LitR Survival Tips and Tricks</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technical Requirements</h3><a id="user-content-technical-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technical Requirements" href="#technical-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This modlist requires the latest version of Fallout 4 on Steam. (1.10.984 as of the time of writing this)</li>
<li>This modlist should be installed on an SSD for performance reasons (the Wabbajack download folder can be on an HDD though).</li>
<li>Recommmended at least 6gb of VRAM.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The modlist is designed for relatively modern, middle range hardware. A high end graphics card is not required, but it does help. There are performance options available, including a <a href="https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/SteamDeck.md">steam deck installation guide</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">If you have less than 6gb of VRAM or the list otherwise performs badly for you</h4><a id="user-content-if-you-have-less-than-6gb-of-vram-or-the-list-otherwise-performs-badly-for-you" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: If you have less than 6gb of VRAM or the list otherwise performs badly for you" href="#if-you-have-less-than-6gb-of-vram-or-the-list-otherwise-performs-badly-for-you"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Do not try to run the list above 1080p, 1440 in fallout is a performance killer</li>
<li>See the steam deck installation guide tweaks (ignore the hard install information), even if you're not running on a steam deck, these performance tweaks can help.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Wabbajack Installation</h2><a id="user-content-wabbajack-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Wabbajack Installation" href="#wabbajack-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/How%20To%20Wabbajack.md">How to Wabbajack</a> for detailed instructions on using Wabbajack to install the modlist</p>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="https://discord.com/channels/885225427839369216/1236112171012718624/1236112171012718624" rel="nofollow">How To Install LitR video tutorial</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><em>This is a large modlist, with several large downloads, including several large sets of textures. Nexus Premium is <strong>highly</strong> recommended for the initial download, expect the initial download and installation to take at least an hour with premium.</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Solving Common Wabbajack Installation Problems</h3><a id="user-content-solving-common-wabbajack-installation-problems" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Solving Common Wabbajack Installation Problems" href="#solving-common-wabbajack-installation-problems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Set your game language to English if you have the game in another language- the installer does not work in other languages (it needs to find and copy the base game video files)</li>
<li>Verify your game files in steam, then run the game through steam, then repeat the installation</li>
<li>Make sure you have at least 300gb free before starting, the modlist needs some extra working space to unpack and repack the archives</li>
<li>If installation fails, and the log has "data error cyclic redundancy check", then you're file paths are too long, try something shorter like "C:\LifeintheRuins"</li>
<li>Unable to download all mods - log out and then back in to the Nexus in the Wabbajack settings</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Additional Setup (post Wabbajack installation)</h2><a id="user-content-additional-setup-post-wabbajack-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Additional Setup (post Wabbajack installation)" href="#additional-setup-post-wabbajack-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Optional Mods and Downloads</h3><a id="user-content-optional-mods-and-downloads" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Optional Mods and Downloads" href="#optional-mods-and-downloads"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Creation Club: If you want to use the creation club paint job support, copy the <a href="https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/CreationClubContent.md">required Creation Club paint jobs</a> files from your <code>fallout4/data directory</code> into the <code>[NODELETE][CC] CreationClub Paint Jobs</code> mod folder, and enable the 5 [CC] tagged mods. Otherwise, you can skip this step.</li>
<li>(Recommended) Download and install into the <code>[NODELETE] Cross Skin Packs</code> (found in the difficulty and customization section),  the following skin packs from <a href="https://gumroad.com/niero" rel="nofollow">https://gumroad.com/niero</a>. They're available for free (use the discount code which can be found on the checkout page), but a donation is suggested. The man makes some fantastic mods, and you can probably afford to buy him a coffee. The links for the 2k version are provided below, however the 4k are also available.
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://niero.gumroad.com/l/fhdhdh" rel="nofollow">Break Action Laser Skin Pack</a></li>
<li><a href="https://niero.gumroad.com/l/mQKCt" rel="nofollow">Cross Cryolance</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Game INI Settings with BethINI</h3><a id="user-content-game-ini-settings-with-bethini" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Game INI Settings with BethINI" href="#game-ini-settings-with-bethini"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Make sure Mod Organizer is not running.  Open BethINI from the <code>Tools</code> folder inside your LitR installation folder.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>Setup</code> tab</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Check that the game path is pointing to the folder called <code>Stock Game Folder</code>, inside your installation folder and not your steam installation</li>
<li>Check that the mod organizer path is pointing to the modorganizer.exe in your installation folder for Life in the Ruins.</li>
<li>Check that your game settings path is set to <code>my documents/my games/fallout 4</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>Basic</code> Tab</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Choose a profile at least one step lower than you would use for vanilla fallout. For most users with less than a 3090 I recommend medium or high, LitR is significantly heavier than vanilla fallout. (The shorter draw distances on medium make A Forest much easier to run, and A Forest makes it so you can't see stuff way in the distance anyway)</li>
<li>For most users, 1920x1080 resolution is recommended.</li>
<li>Enable <code>VSync</code> unless you're using Gsync/FreeSync (the <code>High FPS Physics Fix</code> mod controls VSync and this settings should be ignored, but having it match here doesn't hurt)</li>
<li>On the custom tab, select <code>general</code> in the section drop down, and <code>iNumHWThreads</code> in the settings drop down. Set this to the number of cores your CPU has, doubling that number if it has hyperthreading. For more information on this setting, see <a href="https://stepmodifications.org/wiki/Guide:Skyrim_INI/General#iNumHWThreads" rel="nofollow">https://stepmodifications.org/wiki/Guide:Skyrim_INI/General#iNumHWThreads</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>Details</code> tab</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Field of View (FOV)
It is recommended to leave the FoV vanilla. Setting the FoV higher than 90 has been known to cause weird visual issues with armor mods in the list. It can also effect the pipboy and scopes. Do not use the game console to change the FOV, it will not work.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Nvidia/AMD Control Center</h3><a id="user-content-nvidiaamd-control-center" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Nvidia/AMD Control Center" href="#nvidiaamd-control-center"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Settings here are going to be very system and driver specific, but some general things to be aware of</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>VSync settings MUST be set to application controlled</li>
<li>Disable any framerate caps or limits</li>
<li>Make sure your drivers are up to date.</li>
<li>If you have FreeSync/Gsync enabled and an adaptive sync capable monitor, then you need either enable the 120 FPS NoVSYNC option in the Configuration section, or to make your own version of the HighFPSPhysicsFix configuration ini, to disable vsync and set the FPS cap to your desired value (however, due to the havok engine limitations, 60 or 120 is still recommended).</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mod Organizer Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-mod-organizer-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mod Organizer Configuration" href="#mod-organizer-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Run modorganizer.exe located in the Life in the Ruins installation folder you created.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Video Memory And ENBoost</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the ENB section, are three presets to enable ENBoost 8k, 12k, and 16k, with the required files edited and ready to use, all you have to do is enable one of them. See these videos for help choosing what value works best for you.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y4cz-lFXDo8" rel="nofollow">Introduction to ENBoost</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xSz84F1kgkM" rel="nofollow">How to find your optimal value with ENBoost</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Higher values might work for users with a lot of VRAM, but are unnecessary. For most users this will actually reduce performance and stability. Even with high res textures, FO4 doesn't require that much memory.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">ENBoost is a feature of ENB that allows your FO4 to extend your system's VRAM with your regular RAM. It's not as fast, but it's better than nothing. AMD users with resizable BAR enabled should see even better performance improvements with this setting, and it's recommended to try it out. However this is a HIGHLY system specific setting. What works great for a user with a 3090, will crash for a user with less, which is why it's not turned on for you by default.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If you have issues with textures not loading, stuttering, or the brown face bug, it is recommended to try this.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Difficulty and Customization</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">For People that want to tweak things a little.  Not all options are listed here.  See the section in Mod Organizer for all options</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Lucky 7 - Hardcore Start</code>: You get 7 points to spend at start instead of the regular 24, and get an extra perk point every 7 levels. For players who want a real challenge.</li>
<li><code>Home Unimprovement - Vanilla Crafting</code> : for people who want vanilla settlement</li>
<li><code>Abandoned Hub</code> - an undeground hub settlement, provided as a fast travel alternative</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Configuration</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Additional configuration options</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>120FPS no VSYNC</code>: Enable this mod if you are using a higher refresh rate Gsync/Freesync monitor.  This mod increases the FPS cap from the High Performance Physics Fix mod  and disables vsync.  You can edit the ini file if you need additional changes, or create you own configuration file.</li>
<li><code>Whisky's Tunes</code>: Copyright free music for streamers</li>
<li><code>Nvidia Reflex support</code> and <code>Nvidia Weapon Debris Crash Fix</code>: Enable these if you have an Nvidia card.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Launching the Game and Additional in Game Setup</h2><a id="user-content-launching-the-game-and-additional-in-game-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Launching the Game and Additional in Game Setup" href="#launching-the-game-and-additional-in-game-setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Launch modorganizer.exe from the Life in the Ruins installation folder.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Make sure the drop down next to the Run button says "Play Life in the Ruins"</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Press Run and wait for the game to launch.  Initial launch can take several minutes even on high end systems.  Do NOT press the unlock button. If it seems frozen, try alt-tabbing a couple times.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Start a new survival game (strongly recommended, but not required).  The list is balanced around survival.  There are options in the MCM in game to adjust survival settings and damage settings.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Mod Configuration Menu</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>MCM Settings Manager: Load the LitR Default settings</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Once you're out of the vault, use the Beantown Interiors Settings holotape to enable Hardcore Clutter, and Disable The Mad Bomber's Workshop and Collectibles crafting (these are recommended settings, but aren't required)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Updating the Modlist</h2><a id="user-content-updating-the-modlist" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Updating the Modlist" href="#updating-the-modlist"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before updating the modlist, <a href="https://github.com/WhiskyTangoFawks/LunarFalloutPlus/blob/main/changelog.md">see the full changelog</a> for the latest release. Make sure to follow any additional instructions in the changelog regarding the update process. If an update is marked as save safe, then a new save is not required.</p>
<p dir="auto">To Update the modlist, just rerun the Wabbajack installer with the updated download from the Wabbajack gallery (or prerelease from my Patreon). Check "overwrite" during the installation process.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You do not need to rerun Bethini, as with Life in the Ruins the the game settings are stored in your my documents folder, not inside the list. However, it does no harm to check everything is still setup as expected.</li>
<li>You do need to reapply any MCM settings that you changed. If you're making extensive MCM changes, it is recommended to export these and back them up outside your LitR install before updating.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">If you still have the downloads, Wabbajack will detect them and you will not need to download the entire modlist again, and the process should just take a couple minutes. If you deleted them, then yes, you will need to download all the files again.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Known Issues</h2><a id="user-content-known-issues" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Known Issues" href="#known-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Performance Issues: Infinite Loading Screens, Micro Stuttering, Textures not loading, or the Brown Face bug:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Stop other processes to free up RAM, browser windows are especially a problem here</li>
<li>Try setting the resolution to 1920x1080 if you're running above that</li>
<li>Make sure you've set iNumHWThreads, as specified in the Bethini section of this readme.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>SS2 script failures on new game are the result of going through the opening sequence too quickly. After you finish character creation, wait for 30 seconds or so before exiting the bathroom.</li>
<li>Crashing
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Medal.TV is incompatible with ENB, disable one or the other.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Infinite Loading Screen
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Having your config ini's synced to one-drive. Try setting MO2 to use profile specific INIs in the profile manager dropdown.</li>
<li>Try alt-tabbing a couple times</li>
<li>Make sure you've enabled an ENBoost preset</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Crashlog Scanner</h2><a id="user-content-crashlog-scanner" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Crashlog Scanner" href="#crashlog-scanner"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The list includes the <a href="https://www.nexusmods.com/fallout4/mods/56255" rel="nofollow">Buffout 4 Crashlog Auto Scanner</a>, found inside the tools\Classic Portable folder. To use it simply run the Crash Log Scanner from the dropdown in MO2.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Disable the <code>FCX Mode</code> option in the scanner</li>
<li>Press the Scan Crash Logs button.  The scanner will automatically copy your crash logs over to it's own folder and scan them.  If your crash logs are not in the default location for some reason, you can use the Custom Scan Folder browse button to set the path.</li>
<li>The script will throw a lot of warnings in the <code>CHECKING FOR MODS THAT CAN CAUSE FREQUENT CRASHES...</code>. These can all be safely ignored, I have already dealt with all of them. You do not need to make any modifications to the mod list to deal with CTDs- these are almost always either random instability (which is expected in heavily modded FO4, but should be minimal), mis-configurations on the user end, or modifications that the user has made to the list.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">See the readme.md in the tools\Classic Portable folder for information on how to interpret the results.</p>
